A. Krishnan a male child born to C. Anandan, Hindu and born on 12th May 1986, residing at No. 3/261, Thiruvalluvar
Street, Thelliyar Agaram, Ayyappanthangal, Chennai-600 056, has been living as a female after an elaborate Sexual
Reassignment Surgery on 20th January 2007, Government Kilpauk Medical College Hospital Chennai, Surgery by
Dr. V. Jayaraman, (Regn:32070) Former Professor of Plastic Surgery, Kilpauk Medical College of Head of upgraded Burns
unit, Kilpauk Medical College Hospital Chennai-600 010. By this I May be treated as a Female and henceforth be known
as A. PREETHI.
Chennai,
28th January 2016.

A. KRISHNAN.

Tiruvallur-602 025, has been Living as a Female after an Elaborate Sexual Reassingment Surgery
by Dr. Sivashankar M.S.R.N.O. 603/09, Assistant Surgeon, Govt. Head Quaters Hospital Tiruvallur-602 001. By this I, may
be Treated as a Female and shall henceforth be known as K. MALLIGA.
Tiruvallur
28th January 2016.

P.K. KEERTHI.

Companies Act, 1956 and The Companies (Court) Rules, 1959
Members Voluntary Winding-up
Name of the Company: C-Kam Steel Wire Solutions Private Limited
Cin:U27107TN2010PTC076468
Notice Convening Final Meeting.

Notice is hereby given in pursuance of Section 497 that a Final Meeting of the members of the above named company
will be held at the Registered Office of the company situated at Flat A-14, Ananti Apartments, No. 13/21, Appu Street Second
Lane, Mylapore, Chennai-600 004, on Monday the 7th day of March, 2015 at 10.00 A.M. for the purpose of having an
account laid before them showing the manner in which the winding-up has been conducted and the property of the company
disposed of and of hearing any explanation that may be given by the liquidator and also of determining by a special
resolution of the company, the manner in which the books, accounts and documents of the company and of the liquidator
shall be disposed of.
Chennai,
29th January 2016.

P. SITARAMAN,
